          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<b class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></b>



<br>





tested chrome version:



<span class="line"><!---->tested chrome version:<!----></span>



<br>





Chromium 111.0.5497.0(gs://chromium-browser-asan/linux-release/asan-linux-release-1086812.zip)



<span class="line"><!---->Chromium 111.0.5497.0(gs://chromium-browser-asan/linux-release/asan-linux-release-1086812.zip)<!----></span>



<br>





Chromium 110.0.5478.4



<span class="line"><!---->Chromium 110.0.5478.4<!----></span>



<br>





os version:



<span class="line"><!---->os version:<!----></span>



<br>





22.04



<span class="line"><!---->22.04<!----></span>



<br>





 repro steps:



<span class="line"><!----> repro steps:<!----></span>



<br>





 (1) python3 -m http.server 8000 --dir=|Directory path for containing the crash.html file.|



<span class="line"><!----> (1) python3 -m http.server 8000 --dir=|Directory path for containing the crash.html file.|<!----></span>



<br>





 (2) ./chrome  --disable-gesture-requirement-for-media-playback  --user-data-dir=/tmp/xx --autoplay-policy=no-user-gesture-required --incognito 



<span class="line"><!----> (2) ./chrome  --disable-gesture-requirement-for-media-playback  --user-data-dir=/tmp/xx --autoplay-policy=no-user-gesture-required --incognito <!----></span>





http://localhost:8000/crash.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://localhost:8000/crash.html"><!---->http://localhost:8000/crash.html<!----></a>



<br>





 (3)The crash results may some noisy, such as null-dereference crash or fatal check errors. In this case, manually refreshing the browser several times should trigger  heap buffer overflow.



<span class="line"><!----> (3)The crash results may some noisy, such as null-dereference crash or fatal check errors. In this case, manually refreshing the browser several times should trigger  heap buffer overflow.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





The asan report may also mix with heap buffer overflow and other crash information, such as null-dereference crash or fatal check errors. It seems that this issue may be triggered by other threads crashing beforehand. I am not sure if this is an asan false positive or a valid security issue.



<span class="line"><!---->The asan report may also mix with heap buffer overflow and other crash information, such as null-dereference crash or fatal check errors. It seems that this issue may be triggered by other threads crashing beforehand. I am not sure if this is an asan false positive or a valid security issue.<!----></span>



<br>

Reporter, I noticed that the main() function in crash.html calls itself recursively. Note that DoS attack is not considered as security bugs[1]. Do you have a PoC that doesn't require recursion to trigger this error? Otherwise, I don't think it is a security bug. Keeping it as security bug for now just in case.



<span class="line"><!---->Reporter, I noticed that the main() function in crash.html calls itself recursively. Note that DoS attack is not considered as security bugs[1]. Here's my analysis:



<span class="line"><!---->Here's my analysis:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





# Repro case



<span class="line"><!----># Repro case<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





async function main() {



<span class="line"><!---->async function main() {<!----></span>



<br>





    context = new AudioContext();



<span class="line"><!---->    context = new AudioContext();<!----></span>



<br>





     let node;



<span class="line"><!---->     let node;<!----></span>



<br>





     await context.audioWorklet.addModule(url);



<span class="line"><!---->     await context.audioWorklet.addModule(url);<!----></span>



<br>





     node = new AudioWorkletNode(context, "processor");



<span class="line"><!---->     node = new AudioWorkletNode(context, "processor");<!----></span>



<br>





     await context.resume();                                                        



<span class="line"><!---->     await context.resume();                                                        <!----></span>



<br>





     main()



<span class="line"><!---->     main()<!----></span>



<br>





     context.suspend();



<span class="line"><!---->     context.suspend();<!----></span>



<br>





     context.resume();



<span class="line"><!---->     context.resume();<!----></span>



<br>





 }



<span class="line"><!----> }<!----></span>



<br>





 main();



<span class="line"><!----> main();<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





# Analysis



<span class="line"><!----># Analysis<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The problem is the robustness of context.resume() operation. In Chromium WebAudio, the context state switching from "running" to "suspended" is immediate, but the opposite is not the case; resuming a suspended context is not synchronous since it activates the underlying audio infrastructure. So there's a slight chance of "limbo state" where the platform sink (destination) is running, but the resolution of AudioContext.resume() promise has not happened yet.



<span class="line"><!---->The problem is the robustness of context.resume() operation. In Chromium WebAudio, the context state switching from "running" to "suspended" is immediate, but the opposite is not the case; resuming a suspended context is not synchronous since it activates the underlying audio infrastructure. So there's a slight chance of "limbo state" where the platform sink (destination) is running, but the resolution of AudioContext.resume() promise has not happened yet.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This is usually not a problem, but the thread switching caused by AudioWorklet.addModule() cause invalid thread access. The AudioWorkletGlobalScope should only be accessed from the AudioWorklet thread, but the limbo state makes it possible for non-AudioWorklet thread to execute the code in AudioWorkletProcessor and AudioWorkletGlobalScope. Various problems can be triggered by this and heap-buffer-overflow is just one of them. However, when DCHECK() is enabled the crash can be reproduced consistently at AudioWorkletProcessor::ClonePortTopology() because it is the first operation that allocates memory from the Worklet/Worker space. When that code is executed from non-Worklet thread, DCHECK(global_scope_->IsContextThread()) fails.



<span class="line"><!---->This is usually not a problem, but the thread switching caused by AudioWorklet.addModule() cause invalid thread access. The AudioWorkletGlobalScope should only be accessed from the AudioWorklet thread, but the limbo state makes it possible for non-AudioWorklet thread to execute the code in AudioWorkletProcessor and AudioWorkletGlobalScope. Various problems can be triggered by this and heap-buffer-overflow is just one of them. However, when DCHECK() is enabled the crash can be reproduced consistently at AudioWorkletProcessor::ClonePortTopology() because it is the first operation that allocates memory from the Worklet/Worker space. When that code is executed from non-Worklet thread, DCHECK(global_scope_-&gt;IsContextThread()) fails.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The recursion in the above repro make it easier to crash ASAN by rapidly switching the context status.



<span class="line"><!---->The recursion in the above repro make it easier to crash ASAN by rapidly switching the context status.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





# Resolution



<span class="line"><!----># Resolution<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1) Short-term: BaseAudioContext::NotifyWorkletIsReady() method should handle the suspended case properly so the "limbo state" won't propagate to the platform destination level. POC CL: 



<span class="line"><!---->1) Short-term: BaseAudioContext::NotifyWorkletIsReady() method should handle the suspended case properly so the "limbo state" won't propagate to the platform destination level. POC CL: <!----></span>





http://crrev.com/c/4150813



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://crrev.com/c/4150813"><!---->http://crrev.com/c/4150813<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





2) Long-term: The state switching/resolution logic should be revised so the limbo state doesn't happen. This will require a non-trivial refactoring.



<span class="line"><!---->2) Long-term: The state switching/resolution logic should be revised so the limbo state doesn't happen. This will require a non-trivial refactoring.<!----></span>

Handle a transitory state of context/destination correctly for AudioWorklet operation



<span class="line"><!---->Handle a transitory state of context/destination correctly for AudioWorklet operation<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When the context resumes from a suspended state, it is possible for



<span class="line"><!---->When the context resumes from a suspended state, it is possible for<!----></span>



<br>





the internal (destination) and the external (context) state to be



<span class="line"><!---->the internal (destination) and the external (context) state to be<!----></span>



<br>





different in a rare case. This allows the non-worklet thread to



<span class="line"><!---->different in a rare case. This allows the non-worklet thread to<!----></span>



<br>





touch the worklet-related objects, which can causes invalid access



<span class="line"><!---->touch the worklet-related objects, which can causes invalid access<!----></span>



<br>





to the V8-managed memory space.



<span class="line"><!---->to the V8-managed memory space.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This CL adds a check; if the context state is suspended it swaps



<span class="line"><!---->This CL adds a check; if the context state is suspended it swaps<!----></span>



<br>





the task runner right away without waiting until a resume() promise



<span class="line"><!---->the task runner right away without waiting until a resume() promise<!----></span>



<br>





is resolved.



<span class="line"><!---->is resolved.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;

        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;

          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;

          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
      </style>
      <div class="chops-autocomplete-container">
        <span class="screenreader-hidden" aria-live="polite">
          
        </span>
        <table hidden="">
          <tbody>
            
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    <!----></mr-autocomplete>
            </div>
          </div>

      <style>

 let cl = new ClientLogger("issues");
 if (cl.started("new-issue")) {
 cl.logEnd("new-issue", null, 120 * 1000);
 }
 if (cl.started("issue-search")) {
 cl.logEnd("issue-search");
 }
 }
 });
